- The provided working directory is the only submission surface for this evaluation.
- Do not `git clone`, `git init`, or fetch the target repository into the working directory or any of its subdirectories.

## Required Workflow

1. **Search first** — Use MCP tools to find relevant files and understand existing patterns
2. **Read remotely** — Use `sg_read_file` to read full file contents from Sourcegraph
3. **Edit locally** — Use Edit, Write, and Bash to create or modify files in your working directory
4. **Verify locally** — Run tests with Bash to check your changes

## Tool Selection

| Goal | Tool |
|------|------|
| Exact symbol/string | `sg_keyword_search` |
| Concepts/semantic search | `sg_nls_search` |
| Trace usage/callers | `sg_find_references` |
| See implementation | `sg_go_to_definition` |
| Read full file | `sg_read_file` |
| Browse structure | `sg_list_files` |
| Find repos | `sg_list_repos` |
| Search commits | `sg_commit_search` |
| Track changes | `sg_diff_search` |
| Compare versions | `sg_compare_revisions` |

**Decision logic:**
1. Know the exact symbol? → `sg_keyword_search`
2. Know the concept, not the name? → `sg_nls_search`
3. Need definition of a symbol? → `sg_go_to_definition`
4. Need all callers/references? → `sg_find_references`
5. Need full file content? → `sg_read_file`

## Scoping (Always Do This)

```
repo:^github.com/ORG/REPO$           # Exact repo (preferred)
repo:github.com/ORG/                 # All repos in org
file:.*\.ts$                         # TypeScript only
file:src/api/                        # Specific directory
```

Start narrow. Expand only if results are empty.

## Efficiency Rules

- Chain searches logically: search → read → references → definition
- Don't re-search for the same pattern; use results from prior calls
- Prefer `sg_keyword_search` over `sg_nls_search` when you have exact terms
- Read 2-3 related files before synthesising, rather than one at a time
- Don't read 20+ remote files without writing code — once you understand the pattern, start implementing

## If Stuck

If MCP search returns no results:
1. Broaden the search query (synonyms, partial identifiers)
2. Try `sg_nls_search` for semantic matching
3. Use `sg_list_files` to browse the directory structure
4. Use `sg_list_repos` to verify the repository name

# Kafka Log Retention Policy Configuration Audit

## Your Task

Find all Java source files in apache/kafka that enforce log retention policy: the log.retention.ms and log.retention.bytes validation, the LogManager retention check, and the segment deletion enforcement for both time-based and size-based retention.

## Context

You are working on a codebase task involving repos from the compliance domain.

## Available Resources

The local `/workspace/` directory contains: sg-evals/kafka--0753c489, sg-evals/flink--0cc95fcc, sg-evals/camel--1006f047.


## Output Format

Create a file at `/workspace/answer.json` with your findings in the following structure:

```json
{
  "files": [

  ],

  ],
  "chain": [
    {"repo": "org/repo-name", "path": "relative/path/to/file.go", "symbol": "FunctionName"}
  ],
  "text": "Narrative explanation of your findings, citing repos and file paths."
}
```

Include only the fields relevant to this task. Your answer is evaluated against a closed-world oracle — completeness matters.

- **File recall and precision**: Did you find all relevant files?

7. **`clients/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/common/config/TopicConfig.java`** - Defines `RETENTION_MS_CONFIG` and `RETENTION_BYTES_CONFIG` constants.

## Kafka Log Retention Policy Files

### Configuration Definitions
1. **`server-common/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/server/config/ServerLogConfigs.java`** — Defines `LOG_RETENTION_TIME_MILLIS_CONFIG` (`log.retention.ms`), `LOG_RETENTION_BYTES_CONFIG` (`log.retention.bytes`), and `LOG_CLEANUP_INTERVAL_MS_CONFIG` (`log.retention.check.interval.ms`)

2. **`clients/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/common/config/TopicConfig.java`** — Defines topic-level `RETENTION_MS_CONFIG` and `RETENTION_BYTES_CONFIG`

3. **`server-common/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/server/config/ServerTopicConfigSynonyms.java`** — Maps broker-level `log.retention.*` to topic-level synonyms

### Validation (log.retention.ms and log.retention.bytes)
4. **`core/src/main/scala/kafka/server/KafkaConfig.scala`** — `logRetentionTimeMillis`, `logRetentionBytes`, and `validateValues()` which enforces `log.retention.ms >= 1 || == -1`

5. **`core/src/main/scala/kafka/server/DynamicBrokerConfig.scala`** — `validateLogLocalRetentionMs()` and `validateLogLocalRetentionBytes()` for dynamic config validation

6. **`storage/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/storage/internals/log/LogConfig.java`** — `validateBrokerLogConfigValues()`, `validateRemoteStorageRetentionSize()`, `validateRemoteStorageRetentionTime()`

### LogManager Retention Check
7. **`core/src/main/scala/kafka/log/LogManager.scala`** — Schedules `kafka-log-retention` task; `cleanupLogs()` iterates all logs calling `deleteOldSegments()`

8. **`core/src/main/java/kafka/server/builders/LogManagerBuilder.java`** — Builder that configures `retentionCheckMs`

Contains `cleanupLogs()` method which is the LogManager retention check that calls `deleteOldSegments()` on each log.\n\n4. **`storage/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/storage/internals/log/UnifiedLog.java`** - Contains `deleteOldSegments()`, `deleteRetentionMsBreachedSegments()`, and `deleteRetentionSizeBreachedSegments()` - the actual segment deletion enforcement.\n\n5. **`core/src/main/scala/kafka/server/KafkaConfig.scala`** -
